cur.introTooltipHide = function(success) {

var steps = [
  ['cCountry', "Search by city", "You can narrow the search by entering the place where a person has <b>studied</b>.", 'intr_places_m'],
  ['cCity', "Search by city", "You can narrow the search by entering the place where a person has <b>studied</b>.", 'intr_places_m'],

cur.onSearchChange = function(params) {
  var step = 0;
  if (params['c[country]']) {
    step = 1;
  }
  if (params['c[city]']) {
    step = 2;
  }
  if (params['c[age_from]'] && params['c[age_to]']) {
    step = 3;
  }

  if (step == 3) {
    if (cur.onSearchFinish) return;
    cur.onSearchFinish = cur.showFinalTooltip;
    return cur.introTooltipHide(true);
  }

  if (step > 1 || introStep > 1) {
    introStep = step;
    searchIntroStep();
  } else {
    introStep = step;
  }
}

cur.onSearchPosChange = function(fixed, pos) {

  if (!startPlace || !startPlace.tt) return;
  var t = startPlace.tt.container;
  if (!t) return;
  if (!cur.introTooltipPos) {
    cur.introTooltipPos = getXY(t)[1];
  }
  if (fixed) {
    var top = getXY(ge('filters_td'))[1];
    top = cur.introTooltipPos - top + pos;
    setStyle(t, {
      position: 'fixed',
      top: top + 'px'
    });
  } else {
    setStyle(t, {
      position: 'absolute',
      top: cur.introTooltipPos
    });
  }

  /* can be on start */
  if (fixed && !cur.introTooltipFixed) {
    setTimeout(searchIntroStep, 500);
  }

  setTimeout(searchIntroStep, 0);

  cur.introTooltipFixed = fixed;
  cur.introTooltipFPos = pos;
}

cur.onSearchChange(nav.objLoc);

cur.onSearchStep = function() {
  searchIntroStep();
}

cur.showFinalTooltip = function() {
  cur.searchFriendRow = geByClass1('people_row', ge('results'));

  if (!cur.searchFriendRow) return;

  showTooltip(cur.searchFriendRow, {
    content: '\
  <div id="intr_tt_pointer"></div>\
  <div id="intr_tt">\
    <div id="intr_hide" class="fl_r" onclick="cur.searchFriendRow.tt.hide();" onmouseover="showTooltip(this, {text: \'Hide this notification\', black: 1, shift: [14, 4, 0]})"></div>\
    <div id="intr_header">Go to a user&#39;s page</div>\
    <div id="intr_text">Once you&#39;ve <b>found</b> the right person, click their picture to go to their <b>page</b>.</div>\
    <div class="intr_square intr_profile_m"></div>\
  </div>',
    slideX: -15,
    className: 'profile_intro_side_tt',
    shift: [235, 0, -110],
    forcetodown: true,
    nohide: true,
    nohideover: true
  });
  var tt = cur.searchFriendRow.tt;

  cur.onSearchFinish = function() {
    if (!geByClass1('people_row', ge('results'))) {
      tt.hide();
      delete(cur.onSearchFinish);
    }
  }
}

function searchIntroStep() {
  var s = steps[introStep];

  var shift = [240, 0, -64];

  if (!startPlace) {
    startPlace = ge(steps[introStep][0]);
  }

  if (startPlace && startPlace.tt) {
    var t = startPlace.tt.container;
    var pos = getXY(ge(s[0]));
    cur.introTooltipPos = pos[1] + shift[2] + 29;
    if (cur.introTooltipFixed) {
      var top = getXY(ge('filters_td'))[1];

      if (browser.msie8 || browser.msie7) {
        cur.introTooltipPos += -scrollGetY() + top + top - cur.introTooltipFPos;
      } else {
        cur.introTooltipPos += -scrollGetY() + top - cur.introTooltipFPos;
      }

      top = cur.introTooltipPos - top + cur.introTooltipFPos;
    } else {
      var top = cur.introTooltipPos;
    }
    animate(t, {top: top}, 200);
    ge('intr_header').innerHTML = s[1];
    ge('intr_text').innerHTML = s[2];
    ge('intr_img').className = 'intr_square '+(s[3] || '');

  } else {
    showTooltip(startPlace, {
      content: '\
    <div id="intr_tt_pointer"></div>\
    <div id="intr_tt">\
      <div id="intr_hide" class="fl_r" onclick="cur.introTooltipHide()" onmouseover="showTooltip(this, {text: \'Hide this notification\', black: 1, shift: [14, 4, 0]})"></div>\
      <div id="intr_header">'+s[1]+'</div>\
      <div id="intr_text">'+s[2]+'</div>\
      <div id="intr_img" class="intr_square '+(s[3] || '')+'"></div>\
    </div>',
      slideX: -15,
      className: 'profile_intro_side_tt',
      shift: shift,
      forcetodown: true,
      nohide: true,
      nohideover: true
    });
  }
}


  if (vk.loaded) {
      searchIntroStep()
  } else {
    addEvent(window, 'load', function() {
      searchIntroStep()
    });
  }
}cur.videoMarkSpam = function(link, oid, vid, hash) {
  var loadEl = ce('span', {className: 'loading'});
  ajax.post('/al_video.php', {act: 'video_mark_spam', vid: vid, oid: oid, hash: hash}, {
  onDone: function () {
    link.innerHTML = 'Video marked as spam.';
  },
  showProgress: function () {
    link.parentNode.replaceChild(loadEl, link);
  },
  hideProgress: function () {
    loadEl.parentNode.replaceChild(link, loadEl);
  }});
};
